[10/03/2021 6:56 PM] WilfordGrimley#0124
Hello all. Last Hackathon my team submitted SmartPools, an early decentralized mining solution. 

This team my team will be aiming to produce an on chain music streaming/ library platform where artists can share  their audio NFTs, while (ideally) remaining in possession of the NFTs, and listeners can donate to the artists if they so choose, while building their own music library. 

The project is inspired by FunkWhale, an open source federated music streaming platform for Creative Commons licensed music. 

For the Hackathon I aim to produce a whitepaper and ideally function smart contracts (this should be relatively easy, as the auction house contracts can be adapted). 

In the future, light clients can be constructed that allow listeners to download their library from blockchain. 

It would be lovely to merge my team with any others, or have others join my team. üòÉ

[02/26/2022 5:04 PM] Ergonaut_Alpha#1583
I can only speak personally. but when I look to buy a nft. I and 1) looking at the artwork and asking myself "is this desireable" 2) I am looking for the total supply of a series (I.E. there is only 666 ERGoats) 3) I am looking for added value in the future "is this artist/project committed to maintaining and developing the project to stimulate future demand" I think that a very clever way this is implemented is in the royalties of a NFT. If an artist has placed a royalty % on it to me that give reason for the artist to develop the project because the opportunity of passive income in the future for the artist is there.

lots of fun NFT projects on Ergo right now. you should check them out. if you are looking for a good use case of a "art" forward NFT project I would check out the ergyoroi site. üî• üôÇ

It is worth noting that NFT smart contract technology in its present state does not quite hold up under US copyright law.

Using the SWAMP.AUDIO asset pack minting scheme, assignment provision happens inside the YAML file which tells the smart contract what to do, and the smart contract operates as the trust which carries out the will of the contract holders.
